<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мчаться.html>мча́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mčátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промчаться.html>промча́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promčátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to tear/ sweep <i>(by, past, through)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:промчаться.html>промча́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрела.html>стрело́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>promčátʹsja</b> strelój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dart by; flash by</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(time)</i> to fly by, to frit by</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:мчать.html>мча́ть</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

***промывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промывать.html>промыва́ть</a> (15901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промыть.html>промы́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">promýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промывать.html>промыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промыть.html>промы́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wash <i>(well/properly/thoroughly)</i></li>
<li>to rinse, to bathe, to irrigate</li>
<li>to jig</li>
<li>to wash out, to wash away, to make <i>(a hole, ravine, etc)</i></li></ol>

***промысел.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a> (13921)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prómysel</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>про́мысла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>про́мыслы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>про́мыслов</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">normal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><br />
<strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prómysel</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>про́мысла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>промысла́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>промысло́в</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">professional usage</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>obtainment of resources <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually wild animals, birds, fish</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; hunting, fishing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:охотничий.html>охо́тничий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oxótničij <b>prómysel</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>hunting</b>; game shooting; trapping</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жемчуг.html>же́мчуга</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prómysel</b> žémčuga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pearl <b>fishing</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отхожий.html>отхо́жий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otxóžij <b>prómysel</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">seasonal work <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the <b>hunting</b> or <b>fishing</b> type</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выйти.html>вы́йти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výjti na <b>prómysel</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">go <b>hunting</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыбный.html>ры́бные</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>про́мыслы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rýbnyje <b>prómysly</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">fisheries</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>small-scale handicraft production <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">pottery, forging, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кустарный.html>куста́рный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kustárnyj <b>prómysel</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">handicraft/cottage <b>industry</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> obtainment of something through ill-gotten means
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преступный.html>престу́пный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prestúpnyj <b>prómysel</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">criminal <b>trade/business</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="deprecated-label">usually in the plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> industrial mining enterprise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:горный.html>го́рные</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>про́мыслы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">górnyje <b>prómysly</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mines</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:газовый.html>га́зовый</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:нефтяной.html>нефтяно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gázovyj/neftjanój <b>prómysel</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">oil/gas <b>field</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обустройство.html>обустро́йство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нефтяной.html>нефтяно́го</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>про́мысла</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">obustrójstvo neftjanóvo <b>prómysla</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">construction of surface oil <b>field facilities</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>золоты́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>про́мыслы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zolotýje <b>prómysly</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">gold<b>field</b>s; gold<b>mine</b>s</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соляный.html>соляны́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысл.html>про́мыслы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">soljanýje <b>prómysly</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">salt <b>mine</b>s; salt<b>works</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>providence
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:промысел.html>про́мысел</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:божий.html>бо́жий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prómysel</b> bóžij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">divine <b>providence</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промыть.html>промы́ть</a> (12701)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мыть.html>мыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промыть.html>промы́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промывать.html>промыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wash <i>(well/properly/thoroughly)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жесткий.html>жёсткой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воде́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нельзя.html>нельзя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промыть.html>промы́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v žóstkoj vodé nelʹzjá <b>promýtʹ</b> vólosy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you can't wash your hair properly in hard water</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to rinse, to bathe, to irrigate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попадание.html>попада́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́дует</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обильный.html>оби́льно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промыть.html>промы́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>водо́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pri popadánii v glazá slédujet obílʹno <b>promýtʹ</b> ix vodój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in case of eye contact rinse your eyes in plenty of water</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to jig
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:промыть.html>промы́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:золото.html>зо́лото</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>promýtʹ</b> zóloto</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pan out gold</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wash out, to wash away, to make <i>(a hole, ravine, etc)</i></li></ol>

***промышлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промышлять.html>промышля́ть</a> (14572)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мышля́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-myšljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промышлять.html>промышля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promyšljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to make a living <i>(by)</i>, to support oneself <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:промышлять.html>промышля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:охота.html>охо́той</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>promyšljátʹ</b> oxótoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to earn a livelihood (by) hunting</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:промышлять.html>промышля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевод.html>перево́дами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>promyšljátʹ</b> perevódami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do translations (for a living)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hunt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:промышлять.html>промышля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:белок.html>белку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>promyšljátʹ</b> belku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hunt squirrel</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пронести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пронести.html>пронести́</a> (8546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронести.html>пронести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pronestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проносить.html>проноси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to carry <i>(by, past, through)</i>, to smuggle, to sneak
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пытаться.html>пыта́лся</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронести.html>пронести́</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>еду́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:медсестра.html>медсестра́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остановить.html>останови́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja pytálsja pronestí jej jedú, no medsestrá ostanovíla menjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I tried to sneak her some food, but the nurse stopped me</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пронести.html>пронесло́</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pronesló</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the danger is over!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:еле.html>е́ле</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пронести.html>пронесло́</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jéle <b>pronesló</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">that was close</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to carry with one <i>(for a length of time)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пронести.html>пронесли́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:память.html>па́мять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní <b>proneslí</b> pámjatʹ ob étom čérez vsju žiznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they carried that memory with them for the rest of their lives</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пронести.html>пронести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>века́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pronestí</b> čérez veká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to retain through the centuries</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause (bad) diarrhea
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пронести.html>пронесло́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>pronesló</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his bowels moved; he had diarrhea</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нёс</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронестись.html>пронести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pronestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проноситься.html>проноси́ться</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пронзить.html>пронзи́ть</a> (9876)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронзить.html>пронзи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pronzítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронзать.html>пронза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pierce, to stab, to impale</li>
<li>to run through</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нзи́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:пронзать.html>пронза́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пронз-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***пронизавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пронизать.html>прониза́вший</a> (12789)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***пронизать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пронизать.html>прониза́ть</a> (12789)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">низа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nizátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронизать.html>прониза́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pronizátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронизывать.html>прони́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pierce <i>(through)</i>, to transpierce</li>
<li>to penetrate, to permeate</li>
<li>to run <i>(through)</i></li></ol>

***пронизывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пронизывать.html>прони́зывать</a> (10904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронизать.html>прониза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pronizátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронизывать.html>прони́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pronízyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пронизать.html>прониза́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pierce <i>(through)</i>, to transpierce</li>
<li>to penetrate, to permeate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пронизывать.html>прони́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>косте́й</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тре</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pronízyvatʹ</b> do kostéj (o vétre)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to chill to the marrow</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to run <i>(through)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пронизывать.html>прони́зывает</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éta myslʹ <b>pronízyvajet</b> vsju knígu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">this idea runs through the entire book; the whole book is permeated with this idea</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поэзия.html>поэ́зию</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пронизывать.html>прони́зывает</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грусть.html>грусть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó poéziju <b>pronízyvajet</b> grustʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a feeling of sadness runs through his poetry</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
